Across ^vLzUr7YZ

for each Output-Message in the output message queue of A {
  find every Connection that has a Sender that matches <A, port contained in message> {
    create a new Input-Message that has 
      port ≡ receiver's port
      data ≡ data from message
    enqueue the new message into the input-queue of B
  }
}
 ^aMXQcjKe

 Up ^ODDlyQji

B is a Container and A is one of its children, 
the child's output is promoted to being an output of the Container
find every Connection that has a Sender that matches <B, port contained in message> {
  create a new Output-Message that has 
    port ≡ receiver's port
    data ≡ data from message
  enqueue the new message into the output-queue of A
}
 ^weEyqXGE

"in" ^w3Qhowc5

"xyz" ^tZdWjUJd

Component A ^NZtAMkOR

"out" ^xOYymujt

"xyz" ^RbVzUsmB

Component A ^xR8xgha3

  -->
Through ^ZtV9HmUJ

A is a Container
its' input is passed through to its own output 
(basically, A has been stubbed-out - it doesn't do any processing of messages, it just
 passes them through untouched)
find every Connection that has a Sender that matches <A, port contained in message> {
  create a new Output-Message that has 
    port ≡ receiver's port
    data ≡ data from message
  enqueue the new message into the output-queue of A
}
 ^qy9IrldJ
